				<!-- console.log(homepagedata); -->

				homepagedata.sort(function(a,b){
					return Date.parse(b.order_number) - Date.parse(a.order_number);//倒序
				});
				var homelen = homepagedata.length;
				for(var homei=0;homei<homelen;homei++){
					if(homepagedata[homei].order_number == 15){

						homedata += '<li style="background: '+homepagedata[homei].bg_color+';"><div class="li_in"><a href="'+homepagedata[homei].pic_url+'" target="_blank"><img src="/images/newslide/'+homepagedata[homei].image_path+'" /></a></div></li>';

						var subdata = "";//

										subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status = "报名中";

								}else if(subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status == 1){

								}else if(subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status == 2){
									subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status = "已开班";
								}
								if(subj2 == 0){subtype = "基础班"}else if(subj2 == 1){subtype = "就业班"}
								var openclassdate = subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].openclassdate.substr(0,10);
								clickdata += '<li><a href="javascript:;" class="itcast_click">'+
											'<span>'+subtype+'</span>'+
											'<span>'+openclassdate+'</span>'+
											'<span>'+subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status+'</span>'+
										'</a></li>';
							}
						})(subj2)
						$(".techcon:eq("+subslen+") .techcen_kb").append("<ul>"+clickdata+"</ul>");
					}
					$(".technology_con .techcon .techcen_kb ul").each(function(){
						$(this).children("li").eq(3).css("margin-bottom","15px");
					});
				});
			}
		});
	</script>

		// 数据渲染
		<!-- 首页banner -->
		$.ajax({
			url: "http://www.itcast.cn/newweb/newphoneslide/homepage.json",
			async: false,
			type: "POST",
			success: function(homepagedata){
				<!-- console.log(homepagedata); -->
				var homedata = "";
				homepagedata.sort(function(a,b){
					return Date.parse(b.order_number) - Date.parse(a.order_number);//倒序
				});
				var homelen = homepagedata.length;
				for(var homei=0;homei<homelen;homei++){
					if(homepagedata[homei].order_number == 15){
						homedata += '<li style="background: '+homepagedata[homei].bg_color+';"><div class="li_in"><a href="'+homepagedata[homei].pic_url+'" class="itcast_click"><img src="/images/newslide/'+homepagedata[homei].image_path+'" /></a></div></li>';
					}else{
						homedata += '<li style="background: '+homepagedata[homei].bg_color+';"><div class="li_in"><a href="'+homepagedata[homei].pic_url+'" target="_blank"><img src="/images/newslide/'+homepagedata[homei].image_path+'" /></a></div></li>';
					}
				}
				$(".banner .bd ul").html(homedata);
			}
		});
		<!-- 课程中心 -->
		$.ajax({
			url: "http://www.itcast.cn/newweb/clazzplan/subjects/newwebslide.json",
			async: false,
			type: "POST",
			success: function(subjectsdata){
				<!-- var subdata; -->
				<!-- console.log(subjectsdata); -->
				var subkb = "";
				var sublen = subjectsdata.length;
				var subtype; //就业班还是基础班
				var subarr = arrxueke;//学科的数组
				var subarr2 = arrfenxiao;//分校的数组
				<!-- console.log(subarr); -->
				var subarrlen = subarr.length;
				var layconkec;
				for(arri=0;arri<subarrlen;arri++){
					var subcon = ""; //各学科校区
					var subxks = subjectsdata[""+subarr[arri]+""];
					var s=[];
					
					var subxks2 = Object.keys(subxks);
					
					for(var i=0;i<subarr2.length;i++){
						if(subxks2.indexOf(subarr2[i]) >-1){
							s.push(subarr2[i]);
						}
					}
					subxks2 = s;
					var subxks2len = subxks2.length;
					var subjava;
					for(var subkbi=0;subkbi<subxks2len;subkbi++){
						subjava2 = subxks2[subkbi];
						subjava3 = subjectsdata[""+subarr[arri]+""][""+subjava2+""][2].schoolName;
						subcon += '<li><a href="javascript:;" subd="'+subjava2+'">'+subjava3+'校区</a></li>';
						$(".techcon:eq("+arri+") .xqall ul li").eq(subkbi).children("a").text(subjava3);
					}
					$(".techcon:eq("+arri+") .xqall ul").html(subcon);
					layconkec = $(".techcon").eq(arri).find(".xqall ul li:eq(0) a").attr("subd");
					subjava = subjectsdata[""+subarr[arri]+""][""+layconkec+""];
					for(var subj=0;subj<2;subj++){
						var subdata = "";//
						var subs = subjava[subj][""+subj+""].length;
						if(subs>4) subs = 4;
						if(subs>0){
							(function(subj,subs){
								for(var subi=0;subi<subs;subi++){
									<!-- console.log(subj); -->
									subjava[subj][""+subj+""].sort(function(a,b){
										return Date.parse(a.openclassdate) - Date.parse(b.openclassdate);//正序
									});
									if(subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status == 0){
										subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status = "报名中";
									}else if(subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status == 1){
										subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status = "已爆满";
									}else if(subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status == 2){
										subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status = "已开班";
									}
									if(subj == 0){subtype = "基础班"}else if(subj == 1){subtype = "就业班"}
									var openclassdate = subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].openclassdate.substr(0,10);
									subdata += '<li><a href="javascript:;" class="itcast_click">'+
												'<span>'+subtype+'</span>'+
												'<span>'+openclassdate+'</span>'+
												'<span>'+subjava[subj][""+subj+""][subi].status+'</span>'+
											'</a></li>';
								}
							})(subj,subs)
						}
						$(".techcon:eq("+arri+") .techcen_kb").append("<ul>"+subdata+"</ul>");
					}
					
				}
				
				$(".techcon .xqall ul li").click(function(){
					<!-- console.log($(this).parents(".techcen_right").find(".techcen_kb ul").html()) -->
					$(this).parents(".techcen_right").find(".techcen_kb").stop().animate({"height":0},200,function(){
						$(this).parents(".techcen_right").find(".techcen_kb").stop().animate({"height":255},200);
					})
					subs = $(this).children("a").attr("subd");
					var subslen = $(this).parents(".techcon").index();
					$(".techcon:eq("+subslen+") .techcen_kb").html("");
					subjava = subjectsdata[""+subarr[subslen]+""][""+subs+""];
					for(var subj2=0;subj2<2;subj2++){
						var clickdata = "";
						var subs = subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""].length;
						(function(subj2){
							for(var subi2=0;subi2<subs;subi2++){
								subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""].sort(function(a,b){
									return Date.parse(a.openclassdate) - Date.parse(b.openclassdate);//正序
								});
								if(subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status == 0){
									subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status = "报名中";
								}else if(subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status == 1){
									subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status = "已爆满";
								}else if(subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status == 2){
									subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status = "已开班";
								}
								if(subj2 == 0){subtype = "基础班"}else if(subj2 == 1){subtype = "就业班"}
								var openclassdate = subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].openclassdate.substr(0,10);
								clickdata += '<li><a href="javascript:;" class="itcast_click">'+
											'<span>'+subtype+'</span>'+
											'<span>'+openclassdate+'</span>'+
											'<span>'+subjava[subj2][""+subj2+""][subi2].status+'</span>'+
										'</a></li>';
							}
						})(subj2)
						$(".techcon:eq("+subslen+") .techcen_kb").append("<ul>"+clickdata+"</ul>");
					}
					$(".technology_con .techcon .techcen_kb ul").each(function(){
						$(this).children("li").eq(3).css("margin-bottom","15px");
					});
				});
			}
		});
	</script>
